beginSubroutine: s32'Init_Boss'
  cpuGuardLevelBonus: 0, 80
  storeValue: Mem(CharacterAddAttackRate), Val(10)
  cpuTokuiKyori: 500000
  storeValue: Mem(CharacterAddDefenceRate), Val(75)
  callSubroutine: s32'SkillSet'
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'Init_EX_Boss'
  cpuGuardLevelBonus: 0, 100
  storeValue: Mem(CharacterAddAttackRate), Val(10)
  cpuTokuiKyori: 800000
  storeValue: Mem(CharacterAddDefenceRate), Val(125)
  storeValue: Mem(ExGauge0), Val(12000)
  callSubroutine: s32'SkillSet'
  if: Mem(EXBoss)
    callSubroutine: s32'EX_SkillSet'
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

beginSubroutine: s32'OnFrameStep'
  callSubroutine: s32'cmnOnFrameStep'
  getTrainingItemVal: s32'TRP_ABA02', 2, 157
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(TrainingValue), Val(2)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(0)
      if: Mem(IsEnableNormalAttack)
        checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'CmnActStand'
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
          storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal3), Val(0)
          callSubroutine: s32'Moroha_MeshSetCheck'
        endIf: 
        checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'CmnActStand2Crouch'
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
          storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal3), Val(0)
          callSubroutine: s32'Moroha_MeshSetCheck'
        endIf: 
        checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'CmnActCrouch'
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
          storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal3), Val(0)
          callSubroutine: s32'Moroha_MeshSetCheck'
        endIf: 
        checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'CmnActCrouch2Stand'
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
          storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal3), Val(0)
          callSubroutine: s32'Moroha_MeshSetCheck'
        endIf: 
        checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'CmnActJump'
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
          storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal3), Val(0)
          callSubroutine: s32'Moroha_MeshSetCheck'
        endIf: 
        checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'CmnActJumpPre'
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
          storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal3), Val(0)
          callSubroutine: s32'Moroha_MeshSetCheck'
        endIf: 
        checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'CmnActJumpLanding'
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
          storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal3), Val(0)
          callSubroutine: s32'Moroha_MeshSetCheck'
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
    if: Mem(BattleDoing)
      ifNot: Mem(IsSomebodysCutScene)
        ifNot: Mem(IsRoundTimerStop)
          ifNot: Mem(CheckStop)
            ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal6)
              getTrainingItemVal: s32'TRP_ABA02', 2, 157
              ifOperation: (IS_NOT_EQUAL), Mem(TrainingValue), Val(2)
                ifNot: Mem(EXBoss)
                  modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(20)
                  modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(PlayerVal5), Val(10)
                endIf: 
              endIf: 
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  else: 
    if: Mem(BattleDoing)
      ifNot: Mem(IsSomebodysCutScene)
        ifNot: Mem(IsRoundTimerStop)
          ifNot: Mem(CheckStop)
            modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(12)
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endElse: 
  getTrainingItemVal: s32'TRP_ABA02', 2, 157
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(TrainingValue), Val(2)
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(0)
      if: Mem(IsEnableNormalAttack)
        storeValue: Mem(ExGauge0), Val(1)
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(3000)
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal4), Val(1)
  endIf: 
  else: 
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal4), Val(0)
  endElse: 
  ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal0)
    if: Mem(EXBoss)
      ifNot: Mem(IsRoundTimerStop)
        ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(12000)
          if: Mem(IsLand)
            ifNot: Mem(PlayerDamageOrGuard)
              if: Mem(IsNeutral)
                ifNot: Mem(CheckStop)
                  ifNot: Mem(IsSomebodysCutScene)
                    jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'ABA_SP2'
                  endIf: 
                endIf: 
              endIf: 
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  else: 
    if: Mem(ObjReg4)
      modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg4), Val(-1)
    endIf: 
    ifNot: Mem(CheckStop)
      ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg1), Val(0)
        ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg3), Val(0)
          callPrivateFunction: s32'pala_MorohaFace', 2, 53, 2, 54, 0, 0, 0, 0
          modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg1), Val(1)
          ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(ObjReg1), Val(11)
            storeValue: Mem(ObjReg1), Val(0)
          endIf: 
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg3), Mem(ObjReg2)
        endIf: 
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg3), Val(-1)
      endIf: 
      else: 
        storeValue: Mem(ObjReg3), Val(0)
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(CPUVal0), Val(0)
      modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(CPUVal0), Val(-1)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(CPUVal0), Val(0)
      ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (To3_ENEMY_MAIN_PLAYER), Mem(IsEnemyPlayerDown), Val(1)
        storeValue: Mem(CPUVal0), Val(60)
        modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(4000)
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endElse: 
  ifOperation: (IS_NOT_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Mem(PlayerVal3)
    ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal0)
      walkFSpeed: 4400
      bDashXSpeed: 11500
      bDashYSpeed: 5700
      bDashGravity: 800
      forwardJumpDistance: 6000
      backwardJumpDistance: 4200
      jumpHeight: 35000
      initGravity: 1900
      forwardSuperJumpDistance: 6000
      backwardSuperJumpDistance: 5400
      superJumpHeight: 42000
      superJumpGravity: 1900
      airDashMinimumHeight: 105000
      airFDashTime: 12
      airFDashNoAttackTime: 17
      airBDashTime: 10
      airDashBackVelocity: 15000
      airBDashNoAttackTime: 5
      doubleJumpCount: 1
      airDashCount: 1
      defence: -24
      if: Mem(EXBoss)
        defence: 256
      endIf: 
      guts: 2
      guardBalanceDefence: 32
      guardBalanceTension: 62
      damageWeight: 100
      forwardWalkTension: 5
      forwardJumpTension: 3
      forwardDashTension: 10
      airFDashTension: 5
    endIf: 
    else: 
      walkFSpeed: 10000
      initDashFSpeed: 24500
      fDashAccelSpeed: 770
      fDashFriction: 85
      bDashXSpeed: 16000
      bDashYSpeed: 4000
      bDashGravity: 800
      forwardJumpDistance: 10500
      backwardJumpDistance: 7000
      jumpHeight: 38000
      initGravity: 2500
      forwardSuperJumpDistance: 10500
      backwardSuperJumpDistance: 7000
      superJumpHeight: 52500
      superJumpGravity: 3000
      airDashMinimumHeight: 105000
      airFDashTime: 12
      airFDashNoAttackTime: 17
      airBDashTime: 10
      airDashBackVelocity: 20000
      airBDashNoAttackTime: 5
      doubleJumpCount: 1
      airDashCount: 1
      defence: -24
      guts: 2
      guardBalanceDefence: 32
      guardBalanceTension: 62
      damageWeight: 100
      forwardWalkTension: 5
      forwardJumpTension: 3
      forwardDashTension: 10
      airFDashTension: 5
    endElse: 
  endIf: 
  storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal3), Mem(PlayerVal0)
endSubroutine:

beginState: s32'CmnActFDash'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal0)
      checkCurrentStateEntryName: s32'CmnFDash'
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        setCommonActionMark: 1
        resetDashEasyInput: 
        enableRomanCancelMove: 1
        enableJump: 1
        enableBlock: 1
        enableProximityBlock: 1
        enableBackDash: 1
        enableNormals: 1
        enableSpecials: 1
        enableBurst: 1
        upon: (IDLING)
          addTensionValAtMoveBBS: 12
          ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(9)
            checkInput: (INPUT_ANY_FORWARD)
            ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
              checkInput: (INPUT_HOLD_DASH)
              ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
                clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
                gotoLabelRequests: s32'stop'
              endIf: 
            endIf: 
            checkInput: (INPUT_ANY_BACK)
            if: Mem(Tmp)
              clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
              gotoLabelRequests: s32'stop'
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
        endUpon: 
        upon: (BEFORE_EXIT)
          addInertia: 7000
        endUpon: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    else: 
      callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'cmnFDash', Val(0), Val(0), Val(0), Val(0)
    endElse: 
  endUpon: 
  resetOverwriteLinkBone: 
  gotoLabelIf: s32'Moroha', Mem(PlayerVal2)
  checkCurrentStateEntryName: s32'Cancel_FDash'
  gotoLabelIf: s32'Cancel_FDash', Mem(Tmp)
  commonBankSfx: 0, s32'SE_BTL_CMN_Dash_Sprint_LP', 100
  sprite: s32'aba032_00', 3
  haltMomentum: 1
  endLabel:

  sprite: s32'aba032_02', 3
  createObject: s32'ABA_032_bakeA', (PLAYER)
  createObject: s32'ABA_032_bakeB', (PLAYER)
